    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Here, you will find the number, weight and size limits-plus excess baggage fees-for checked baggage on ANA flights.</p>
<ul>
<li>Excess baggage fees will apply when checking in most baggage that exceeds the free baggage allowance. See Excess Baggage Fees.</li>
</ul>

<li>When traveling on Japanese domestic sectors using a ticket for which the International Conditions of Carriage apply, the baggage rules for international flights will apply.</li>
<li>Please be advised that in the event that it is impossible to confirm whether or not an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>

<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p><strong>Notes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>The total linear dimensions (length + width + height) of the item cannot be more than 62 inches (158 cm), including wheels and handle.</li>
<li>Bags must be checked in at the check-in counter in the departure lobby or at a self-service machine.</li>
<li>If your itinerary includes a flight by another airline, that airline's baggage rules may also apply. This includes codeshare flights-the joint operation of an aircraft by two or more carriers. Find out more about <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/codeshare/">baggage on codeshare flights</a></strong>.</li>
<li>The <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/free-baggage-allowance/">free baggage allowance</a></strong> written on the flight ticket will apply.</li>
<li>When traveling in Premium Economy on Japan domestic sectors, the free baggage allowance for First Class will apply.<ul>
<li>When traveling in Economy Class, the allowance for Premium Economy and Economy Class will apply.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                How to Increase Baggage Allowances
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Some ANA Mileage Club members enjoy additional free checked bags and fewer weight restrictions. For details, please see <strong><a href="/en/us/amc/premium-members/">Premium Member Benefits</a></strong>.</p>
<p>ANA Mileage Club members may use miles to increase the number of bags. For details, please see <strong><a href="/en/us/amc/additional-baggage-allowance/">Additional Baggage Allowance</a></strong>.</p>
<p>Not a member yet? Join the <a href="https://cam.ana.co.jp/amcmember/amcentry/AMCEntryFacadeEn" target="_blank" class="icon-blank"><strong>ANA Mileage Club</strong><img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Bags for Young Children
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>If you're traveling with a child younger than 2 who does not occupy their own seat, one additional piece of baggage can be checked in on top of your allowance. The size and weight of the additional piece should conform to normal bag rules; otherwise excess baggage fees may be incurred.</p>
<p>Baggage guidelines for children occupying their own seat are the same as for adult passengers.</p>
<p>Find out about carrying on strollers, see <a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/carry-on/"><strong>Carry-On Items</strong></a></p>
<p>Find out about checking in strollers and other details about <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/expectant-mothers-and-children/#anchor-families-with-children">traveling with children</a></strong>.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Self-Service Baggage Drop Machines
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Self-service machines are available at some airports. Passengers who have checked in and have a boarding pass can go directly to a self-service machine to check in their bags.</p>
<p>However, these customers should proceed to an ANA check-in counter for international flights:</p>
<ul>
<li>Those requiring boarding assistance</li>
<li>Those required to pay excess baggage fees</li>
<li>Those checking in dangerous, fragile, and non-standard baggage. Additionally, golf bags, skis or snowboards, surfboards, pets, strollers, umbrellas or tripods cannot be checked in at a self-service kiosk.</li>
</ul>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* Depending on reservation and ticket details, some passengers may not be able to use this service. Consult ANA ground staff for details.</li>
<li>* Due to system specifications, baggage tags may not be issued to the final destination if you are not checked in for the connecting flight. Please ask an ANA ground staff for details.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you have printed a baggage tag on a self-service check-in machine, attach the tag to your bag, then check it in using the self-service baggage drop machine. (These guidelines may differ by airport.)</p>
<p>On top of items not permitted in checked baggage (see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/">Restricted and Banned Items</a></strong>) fragile items and baggage of non-standard shape cannot be checked in using self-service machines.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Hours of Operation for Self-service Baggage Drop Machines
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1501 aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--small--none aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn--medium--12 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--small--0 aem-GridColumn--default--8 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0">
<!-- ANA-1501  -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">

<!--  ANA-1501 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                For Passengers Using Wheelchairs
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Since cabin storage space is limited, we ask that you check your wheelchair at the check-in counter and use ANA's wheelchair service. We will provide an attendant to assist you in moving to your seat, and our aircrafts are equipped with a cabin wheelchair for your convenience on board.</p>
<ul>
<li>Please let us know if you prefer to use your own wheelchair to/from the aircraft.</li>
<li>We can accept one manually operated, foldable wheelchair per flight for all international routes.</li>
<li>For details such as size and flight eligibility, please check with ANA airport staff. Please note that in some cases, due to limited storage space, we may not be able to accommodate storage of a wheelchair.</li>
<li>For more information, please see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/customers-with-disabilities/">Travelers with Disabilities</a></strong>.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Electric Wheelchairs
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>If you use an electric wheelchair, please let us know the size, weight and type of battery when you book your flight. Also, please check in at least 120 minutes prior to your departure.</p>
<p>There are certain limitations by law for checking in/carrying on electronically powered wheelchairs equipped with lithium ion batteries.</p>
<p>Please see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/">Restricted and Banned Items</a></strong>&nbsp;for details about lithium ion batteries.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                More Checked Baggages Notes
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>Shut down any electronic devices before you place them in checked baggage.</li>
<li>Baggage is handled with considerable care, but if it happens to be damaged due to an inherent defect or property, ANA will not be liable. See <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/damage-lost/">Damaged, Lost and Left-Behind Items</a></strong>&nbsp;for more.<br>
Furthermore, ANA will not be liable for any damage or loss that may occur, so please do not check fragile items such as watches and glass, electronic devices such as computers and cameras, valuables, or daily necessities such as medicine onto the airplane.</li>
<li>The checked bags of passengers arriving in or departing from the United States may be opened for inspection.<ul>
<li>More info is available from the <strong><a href="https://www.tsa.gov/travel/security-screening#quickset-security_screening_quicktabs_1" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">US Transportation Security Administration<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

                <div id="anchor-excess-baggage-fees-contents" class="cp-tab-contents" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="anchor-excess-baggage-fees">
                    
                    <div class="res-contents cp-container">
                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Excess Baggage Fees
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Excess baggage fees will apply to items that do not meet Checked Baggage Guidelines.</p>
<ul>
<li>If more than one limit is exceeded, the sum of all fees applies.</li>
<li>Applicable currency and fees may vary depending on where the baggage is checked in.<ul class="none-style">
<li>* However, different fees may apply to itineraries which are subject to <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/codeshare/#anchor-usca-baggage-provisions">U.S. or Canadian laws and regulations</a></strong>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>The currency and fee applied vary depending on the itinerary, the sector on which baggage is checked in, as well as the airport at which the payment is made.</p>
<p>Currency details:</p>
<ul>
<li>When paying in the US: The USD amount applies.</li>
<li>When paying in Canada: The CAD amount applies.</li>
<li>When paying in Japan: The JPY amount applies.</li>
<li>When paying in Germany, France, Belgium, Austria and Russia: The EUR amount applies.</li>
<li>When paying in the UK: The EUR amount applies, converted to GBP</li>
<li>When paying anywhere else: The USD amount applies, converted to the currency of the country of departure.<ul class="none-style">
<li>* <strong><a href="/en/us/amc/additional-baggage-allowance/">Use miles</a></strong> to pay excess baggage charges on ANA international flights.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Fees differ depending on the route.</p>
<ul>
<li>Area 1: North America, South and Central America, Hawaii</li>
<li>Area 2: Europe, Africa, Middle East</li>
<li>Area 3: Asia (including Japan), Oceania</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1607 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

    </div>

<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>To save time at the airport, you can pay excess baggage fees for one bag during the booking process, but only for international flights with these conditions:</p>
<ul>
<li>Flight tickets must have a ticket number starting with 205</li>
<li>The itinerary must not include US or Canadian cities</li>
<li>You cannot prepay baggage fees if your booking:<ul>
<li>Includes codeshare flights-the joint operation of an aircraft by two or more carriers-or flights operated by another airline</li>
<li>Is for travel within Japan</li>
<li>Is on a separately printed flight ticket</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--small--12 aem-Grid--default--12 aem-Grid--medium--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Checking in Bulky, Oversized and Fragile Items
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Oversize Baggage
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Bags with total linear dimensions (length + width + height, including wheels and handle) that exceed 80 inches (203 cm) but are less than 115 inches (292 cm) can be checked in provided they can be loaded in the cargo compartment of the aircraft used.</p>

    </div>

        <div class="res-contents ana2_bgcolor_ui-01">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Customers departing for/from Vienna, London Heathrow, Brussels, ,Paris, Phnom Penh, Chennai, Wuhan or Australia (Sydney, Perth) airports
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>The weight of checked baggage is limited to 32 kg per piece. Please make sure that each piece of baggage is packed so that it does not exceed 32 kg.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

        
    </div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Maximum Baggage Length by Aircraft Type
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1501 aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--small--none aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn--medium--12 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--small--0 aem-GridColumn--default--6 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0">
<!-- ANA-1501  -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="table-responsive res-contents">
      <table class="table"><thead><tr><th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Aircraft Types</strong></th>
<th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Maximum Baggage Length</strong></th>
</tr></thead>
<tbody><tr><td>781 (Boeing 787-10)</td>
<td>98 inches (250 cm)</td>
</tr><tr><td>789 (Boeing 787-9)</td>
<td>98 inches (250 cm)</td>
</tr><tr><td>788 (Boeing 787-8)</td>
<td>98 inches (250 cm)</td>
</tr><tr><td>320 (Airbus A320)</td>
<td>102 inches (260 cm)</td>
</tr><tr><td>DH8 (De Havilland Canada Dash 8-400)</td>
<td>70 inches (180 cm)</td>
</tr><tr><td>CR7 (Bombardier CRJ700)</td>
<td>98 inches (250 cm)*</td>
</tr><tr><td>DH2 (De Havilland Canada Dash 8-200)</td>
<td>63 inches (160 cm)</td>
</tr></tbody></table>

    </div><!-- / table-responsive -->
</div>
<!--  ANA-1501 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul class="none-style">
<li>* Height cannot exceed 25.5 inches (65 cm); width can't exceed 41.3 inches (105 cm) or less.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Notes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Please <strong><a href="/en/us/help/">Contact ANA by phone</a></strong>&nbsp;as early as possible to check if your bulky baggage can be checked in.</li>
<li>In the event that it is impossible to confirm if an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                High-Value Items
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Please do not check in highly valuable items such as cash, jewelry, securities, artwork, antiques and other valuables, as ANA cannot be responsible for damage to or loss of such items.</p>
<p>When traveling on US flights, the DOT rule, <a href="https://www.transportation.gov/sites/dot.gov/files/docs/webnotice_04012009_rg_0.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf"><strong>Guidance on Airline Baggage Liability and Responsibilities of Codeshare Partners Involving International Itineraries</strong><img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a>, applies.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Fragile Items
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Fragile items such as clocks, cameras, personal computers, bottles, and glass products can be checked as long as they meet size and weight requirements.</p>
<p>Considerable care is taken with the handling of baggage, but if fragile items, such as ceramics, glass products, or alcohol, are damaged due to an inherent defect or property, ANA will not be liable. Please do not check in highly fragile items, as ANA cannot be responsible for damage to or loss of such items.</p>
<p>When traveling on US flights, the DOT rule, <strong><a href="https://www.transportation.gov/sites/dot.gov/files/docs/webnotice_04012009_rg_0.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf">Guidance on Airline Baggage Liability and Responsibilities of Codeshare Partners Involving International Itineraries<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a></strong>&nbsp;applies.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Electronic Devices
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Electronic devices (personal computers, cameras, etc.) can be checked in as long as they meet size and weight requirements. Shut down any electronic devices before you place them in checked baggage.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Musical Instruments
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Musical instruments, such as guitars and violins, can be checked in as part of your baggage allowance as long as they meet size and weight requirements.</p>
<p>Oversized items whose dimensions are more than 203 cm (80 in.) but not larger than 292 cm (115 in.) can be checked in, but are subject to excess baggage fees.</p>
<ul>
<li>These can be checked in as long as they can be loaded into the aircraft's cargo compartment. Please <strong><a href="/en/us/help/">contact ANA</a></strong>&nbsp;as early as possible to determine if your instrument can be checked.</li>
<li>If it is impossible to confirm if an item can be transported before the departure time, the request may be rejected.</li>
<li>Items that exceed 292 cm (115 in.) or whose weight exceeds 45 kg (99 lbs.) cannot be checked in. You should contact a cargo carrier.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Bicycles &amp; Other Sporting Equipment
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>The following Sporting Equipment will be checked in free of charge if the quantity and weight are within a free Checked Baggage allowance of your boarding class.</p>
<ul>
<li>Bicycles</li>
<li>Surfboards</li>
<li>Golf bags</li>
<li>Fishing equipment</li>
<li>Diving equipment</li>
<li>Rackets</li>
<li>Ski/snowboarding equipment*</li>
</ul>
<p>etc.</p>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* Please note that if skis, poles, snowboards, shoes and other ski equipment are packed individually, an excess charge will apply per piece.</li>
</ul>
<p>If the free baggage allowance is exceeded, excess baggage fees will apply.<br>
Please note that handling exceeding size (the total linear dimensions) is only different from regular baggage.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1501 aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--small--none aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn--medium--12 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--small--0 aem-GridColumn--default--6 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0">
<!-- ANA-1501  -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="table-responsive res-contents">
      <table class="table"><thead><tr><th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Size Limit *The total linear dimensions (length + width + height)</strong></th>
<th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Aplicable Allowance</strong></th>
</tr></thead>
<tbody><tr><td>Exceed 158 cm (62 in.) to 292 cm (115 in.) or less</td>
<td>No excess baggage fees apply</td>
</tr><tr><td>Exceed 292 cm (115 in.)</td>
<td>Not acceptable</td>
</tr></tbody></table>

    </div><!-- / table-responsive -->
</div>
<!--  ANA-1501 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>It may not be possible check in large pieces of sporting equipment for some aircraft types due to limited loading space. Please see Restrictions by Aircraft Type above.</li>
<li>Please <strong><a href="/en/us/help/">contact ANA</a></strong>&nbsp;as early as possible to determine if your equipment can be checked. If it is impossible to confirm before the departure time if an item can be transported, the request may be rejected.</li>
<li>If a bicycle is not packaged or protected, or the packaging is not suitable or adequate, ANA cannot be responsible for damage.</li>
<li>Except for electric bicycles, electric vehicles cannot be carried on board or checked in.<br>
Please note that there are certain conditions for the transportation of electric bicycles. Please refer to <a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/#anchor-restriction-battery-powered-devices"><strong>"General electronic devices with or without a built-in lithium battery"</strong></a> beforehand.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">

    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h2 class="type--header-2 ">
              
                Information for Carry-On Items and Onboard Rules
              
            </h2>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Here, you'll find guidelines for carry-on baggage and other items, and the use of such items onboard the aircraft.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1608 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1608  -->


    <div class="res-contents cp-container cp-tab-container">
        <div class="cp-tabset cp-tabset-default">
            <div class="cp-tab-menu-box">
                <button class="cp-pulldown-select-txt cp-tab-select-txt">
                    <span class="cp-pulldown-ttl">SELECT</span>
                    <i class="cp-pulldown-btn">
                        <img src="/common-layout/images/ico_pull_open.png" alt="Open" class="cp-open-btn">

                    </i>

                  <button class="cp-tab-btn cp-tab-btn-prev" aria-label="Previous"><span class="invisible" lang="en">prev</span></button>
                  <ul class="cp-tab-menu-list" role="tablist">
                      <li>
                          <a href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-carry-on-items" aria-controls="anchor-carry-on-items-contents" class="cp-tab-menu-btn is-selected" tabindex="-1" role="tab" aria-selected="true">

            <div class="cp-tab-contents-list">
                
                <div id="anchor-carry-on-items-contents" class="cp-tab-contents is-selected" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="true" aria-labelledby="anchor-carry-on-items">
                    
                    <div class="res-contents cp-container">
                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 aem-Grid--large--12 aem-Grid--medium--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Guidance for Carrying on Baggage and Other Items
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--offset--large--0 aem-GridColumn--large--none aem-GridColumn--medium--12 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12 aem-GridColumn--large--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Most travelers can bring on board one full-size carry-on bag and one personal item (handbag, umbrella, camera, etc.).</p>
<ul>
<li>If your itinerary includes a flight by another airline, that airline's baggage rules may also apply. This includes codeshare flights—the joint operation of an aircraft by two or more carriers—that operate using ANA flight numbers. For details, see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/codeshare/">Codeshare Baggage Information</a></strong>.</li>
<li>When traveling on Japanese domestic sectors using a ticket for which the International Conditions of Carriage apply, the baggage rules for international flights will apply.</li>
<li>Please be advised that in the event that it is impossible to confirm whether or not an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>
<li>A baggage within the size specified below may be included in checked baggage when the size is not suited for the cabin. Please check in any baggage (carrying bag, baby stroller, jute bag, etc.) exceeding the following size.</li>
<li>If you carry on board any baggage exceeding the carry-on baggage allowance, it may cause delay or cancellation of your flight. For a Comfortable and Safe Journey, please check in baggage exceeding the permitted size for carry-on baggage before passing through security.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Size and Weight Limits
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Carry-on baggage is limited to what can be stored in the overhead compartment or under the seat in front of you. It cannot exceed these limits:</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-0003 image aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-0003 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="img-align-center">
        <figure>
            <div>
                
                <img src="/www2/travel-information/baggage-information/carry-on/size-and-weight-limits-image_en.jpg" alt="">
            </div>
            
        </figure>
    </div>
</div>
<!--/ANA-0003 -->


    

</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1612 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1612 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
            <div class="layout-grid" role="list">
            <div class="layout-grid-section-column3" role="listitem">
                


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Weight Limit
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>No more than 22 lbs. (10 kg), including one personal item</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

            </div>
        
            <div class="layout-grid-section-column3" role="listitem">
                


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Size Limit
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Total linear dimensions (length + width + height) cannot exceed 45 in. (115 cm)</p>
<ul>
<li>The dimensions of each side cannot exceed 22 x 16 x 10 in. (55 cm x 40 cm x 25 cm)</li>
<li>Includes wheels and handle</li>
</ul>
<p>In the case of the aircraft on Japan Domestic Flights which has seating capacity of less than 100 (DH8/DH2/CR7 aircraft types)</p>
<p>Total linear dimensions (length + width + height) cannot exceed 39 in. (100 cm)</p>
<ul>
<li>The dimensions of each side cannot exceed 18 x 14 x 8 in. (45 cm x 35 cm x 20 cm)</li>
<li>Includes wheels and handle</li>
</ul>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* Even if the size of each side is within the regulations, if the sum of the three sides exceeds the regulations, the item cannot be brought in.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

            </div>
        
            <div class="layout-grid-section-column3" role="listitem">
                


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Number of Pieces
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Up to one piece per passenger.</p>
<ul>
<li>Aside from personal belongings (handbag, camera, umbrella, etc.), one piece of baggage that meets the criteria below is allowed.</li>
<li>Includes souvenirs or items you purchased.</li>
<li>Star Alliance Gold members travelling across two or more member carriers are still limited to one carry-on baggage.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

            </div>
        </div>
    </div>


    

</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Notes:
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>Depending on the aircraft type and the size of the storage space, some items may not be accepted for carry-on even if they meet size and weight limits.</li>
<li>Large tripods: Tripods longer than 60 cm (approx. 23.6 inches) when folded cannot be carried on board.</li>
<li>An additional seat must be purchased if the size of your carry-on exceeds the carry-on limit.<ul>
<li>If you wish to bring a contrabass into the cabin, it will be accepted in economy class.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>In the event that it is impossible to confirm whether or not an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>
<li>Please see the gate agent or <a href="/en/us/help/"><strong>contact ANA by phone</strong></a> if you have a question about whether an item can be carried on board.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 id="anchor-liquids-aerosols-gels" class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Carrying on Liquids, Aerosols and Gels
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>All liquids, aerosols, and gels (LAGs), must be carried in containers with a capacity no larger than 3.4 oz or 100 ml each.</p>
<p>Containers with a larger capacity, even if the content are less than 3.4 oz., must be placed in the checked baggage.</p>
<p>Those containers must be placed in a transparent, resealable plastic bag (zip-locked bag) with a volume no larger than one liter (1,000 ml), and a two side total no larger than 40 cm. The containers must fit into the bag which must be completely closed.</p>
<p>Some countries/regions may restrict other items in addition to those below from being carried on board and checked in. <a href="/en/us/travel-information/airport-and-city-info/"><strong>See Airport and City Information</strong></a> for more information.</p>
<p>LAGs purchased at duty-free shops, etc., at the departure airport can be carried on board. However, the following requirements may apply depending on the country. For details, see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/#anchor-restrictions-duty-free">Duty-Free LAG Items</a></strong>.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--small--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Size guidelines
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--6 aem-Grid--small--12 aem-Grid--default--6 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-0003 image aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--default--6">

<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn--small--none aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--small--0 aem-GridColumn--default--6 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>For square bags: length within 20 cm x width within 20 cm</li>
<li>For rectangular bags: combined length and width no longer than 40 cm</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Exceptions to Liquids Rules
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Medications, baby milk and baby food, and food for special dietary needs can be carried on board without placing them in a transparent plastic bag.</p>
<ul>
<li>For medication, a copy of the prescription or a medical certificate issued by a medical practitioner indicating the name of the illness, etc., may be requested at security.</li>
<li>Breast milk and baby food is only permitted for passengers traveling with an infant.<ul>
<li><strong>Departures from the United States:</strong> Breast milk (but not baby food) may be carried on board even when an infant is not traveling with the passenger. It must be presented to inspectors at the security checkpoint.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Departures from Thailand
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Only hand sanitizers can be carried on board up to 350 ml per container.Please be aware that if you transfer to an international flight after arriving in Japan, a liquid containing more than 100 milliliters per container cannot be carried on board.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Departing from the UK
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>Strictly enforced by the authorities.<br>
If restricted items are found, baggage will be opened and re-inspected by security staff. It may take more time to complete inspections, especially during the year-end and New Year holidays.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1613 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1613 -->

    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
            
            
                <dl>
                    
                        <dt>
                            <strong>Notes</strong>
                        </dt>
                        <dd>
                            <ul>
<li>Please place your PC, tablet, and/or liquids flat on the tray. Do not place them on top of other items.</li>
<li>Please confirm in advance that the zipper of the transparent plastic bag for liquids can be closed.<br>
If the zipper does not close and/or there are items that do not fit, they will be thrown away.<ul class="none-style">
<li>* Please note that ANA Business Class and First Class amenity kits also contain liquids.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

                        </dd>
                    
                </dl>
            
            
            
        </div>
    </div>


    

<!--/ANA-1613 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Eligible Flights
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>The rules apply to flights departing from the following countries.</p>
<ul>
<li>International routes only: Japan, Korea, Taiwan, Hong Kong, Vietnam, China, Singapore, Indonesia, Philippines, Myanmar.</li>
<li>International routes and domestic routes (flights within the EU): EU member states*1, United Kingdom, United States, Mexico, Thailand, India, Canada, Mainland China, Philippines, Cambodia.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-0102-1 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-0102-1-->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cp-container cp-list-container">
        <ul role="list" class="list-note-num list-mt-normal">
            <li role="listitem">
				
                	<span class="note-num">*1.</span><div class="note-des">27 EU member countries<br>
Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Croatia, Republic of Cyprus, Czech Republic, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, France, Germany, Greece, Hungary, Ireland, Italy, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Netherlands, Poland, Portugal, Romania, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, and Sweden.<br>
The non-EU members Iceland, Switzerland, and Norway apply the same rules.</div>
                
                
                
            </li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-0102-1 -->


    

</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Strollers and Child Seats
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Folding strollers, portable cradles, and child seats can be checked in free of charge as long as they are for the use of the traveler who checks them.</p>
<p>Baby strollers can be brought on board only if they fall within the above size regulations when folded.</p>
<ul>
<li>As only one item of carry-on baggage is allowed per passenger, passengers bringing a baby stroller on board cannot bring another carry-on item, aside from personal items such as a handbag, camera or umbrella.</li>
<li>Please fold and store your baby stroller in a case before passing through the ticket gate. If you do not have a case of your own, our staff will provide you with a plastic bag specifically for use with baggage.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Find out more about <a href="/en/us/travel-information/expectant-mothers-and-children/#anchor-families-with-children"><strong>Traveling With Children</strong></a>.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Carrying Medical Equipment on Board
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>If you need to travel with medication, medical equipment or devices, such as CPAP machines, or hearing aids that emit radio waves, please contact the <a href="/en/us/travel-information/customers-with-disabilities/"><strong>ANA Disability Desk</strong></a> in advance to confirm if the item is permitted onboard.</p>
<ul>
<li>Be prepared to provide the manufacturer, product name, model, size, battery type, etc.</li>
<li>Please note that we may check your equipment again at the airport before departure.</li>
</ul>
<p>Note: Scissors, even those that are part of medical equipment, cannot be carried on board.</p>
<p><strong>Also see:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/en/us/travel-information/customers-with-disabilities/medical-requirements/"><strong>Medications and Medical Devices</strong></a></li>
<li><a href="/en/us/travel-information/customers-with-disabilities/medical-requirements/medical-oxygen-cylinders/"><strong>Passengers Using Oxygen</strong></a></li>
<li><a href="/en/us/travel-information/customers-with-disabilities/medical-requirements/"><strong>Passengers Using CPAP Machines</strong></a></li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

                    </div>
                </div><!-- / cp-tab-contents -->
            
                
                <div id="anchor-onboard-information-contents" class="cp-tab-contents" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="anchor-onboard-information">
                    
                    <div class="res-contents cp-container">
                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--small--12 aem-Grid--default--12 aem-Grid--medium--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Onboard Information
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Storing Carry-On Items
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Please store carry-on baggage in the overhead compartment or under the seat in front of you to ensure a safe journey. Leaving baggage where it might hinder an emergency evacuation such as in the aisle or near the emergency exits is prohibited by law. Passengers seated where there is no seat in front of them are always required to keep the area around their feet free of baggage.</p>
<p>When storing your baggage in the overhead compartment, please make sure everything is stored neatly. Baggage that is not secured properly could fall out and injure you or other passengers.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Restrictions on Smoking
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Smoking and/or the use of fire in all seats, including the restrooms, is strictly prohibited. If a fire is started and the fire detector is activated, the aircraft will need to turn back to the gate or make an emergency landing at a nearby airport.</p>
<p><strong>E-cigarettes, Non-combusted cigarettes</strong>&nbsp;should be carried on the aircraft, but they cannot be used onboard. They cannot be in checked baggage.</p>
<ul>
<li>Because smokeless cigarettes may impair the comfort of other passengers, the ANA Group prohibits their use onboard. In addition, it is prohibited to charge e-cigarettes, non-combusted cigarettes, and spare rechargeable batteries onboard.</li>
<li>One lighter or one small box of safety matches per person can be carried on board.<ul>
<li>Please make sure not to leave your lighter in the cabin.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Lighters containing oil tanks, cigar lighters and pre-mixed burner lighters (turbo lighters, jet lighters, lighters producing a blue flame, etc.) are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</li>
</ul>
<p>There may be occasions where passengers will not be allowed to take these items on board due to country rules and regulations. Please see <a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/"><strong>Restricted and Banned Items</strong></a> for details.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Electronic Devices Emitting Radio Waves
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Electronic devices that emit radio waves (including cell phones, laptops and electronic gaming consoles) are not permitted to be used for communication from the time the doors close before departure to the time the aircraft arrives at the destination gate.</p>
<p>Please set your device to airplane mode (sometimes called standalone mode, offline mode or flight mode), which blocks the sending and receiving of radio waves for functions that include phone calls, emails, text messages, and internet access.</p>
<p>The cabin attendants will make announcements to notify passengers when they can and cannot use these items.</p>
<p><strong>Phones Requiring Special Caution, Such as Cell Phones for Children</strong></p>
<p>Some phones turn on periodically to send their position even when the power is turned off. Please turn the power off completely to assure it does not interfere with aircraft function.</p>
<ul>
<li>Examples: Kids' PHONE™ by NTT DOCOMO (FOMA SA800i/F801i) or Junior Phone by au (K001/mamorino/mamorino2/mamorino3)</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-0003 image aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--small--none aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--small--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--small--0 aem-GridColumn--default--3 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0 aem-GridColumn--medium--6">
<!-- ANA-0003 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    
        <figure>
            <div>
                <img src="/www2/travel-information/baggage-information/carry-on/wifi.jpg" alt="electronic devices emitting radio waves">
                
            </div>
            
        </figure>
    
</div>
<!--/ANA-0003 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Bluetooth and Wi-Fi Connections
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Connections between Bluetooth devices (e.g., wireless headphones) and connections between Wi-Fi devices (electronic game consoles) are permitted at all times as long as the device is set to airplane mode.</p>
<p>Note that since wireless communication is restricted to that occurring within the aircraft, connecting to mobile Wi-Fi routers or public wireless LAN is prohibited.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

                <div id="anchor-missing-baggage-contents" class="cp-tab-contents" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="anchor-missing-baggage">
                    
                    <div class="res-contents cp-container">
                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                What to Do if Your Baggage Is Missing
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>We handle passengers' checked baggage with great care, but there may be times when your baggage does not reach its destination. We sincerely apologize to these passengers; we will work hard to resolve the situation.</p>
<p>If you are not able to find your bag at the arrival airport, please report your missing baggage immediately by using one of the following methods to file your report;</p>
<ul>
<li>Report via delayed baggage self-service portal<br>
<strong><a href="https://mybag.aero/ana/delayed" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">Delayed baggage report<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong></li>
<li>Contact baggage service desk at the arrival airport</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Declaration Deadline for Missing Luggage
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>As indicated in <strong><a href="/en/us/conditions-of-carriage/">the International Conditions of Carriage</a></strong>, a declaration of missing baggage must be submitted within 21 days from the day after the day on which the baggage was to be received (in the case of a delay) or the day on which the baggage could have been received (in the case of loss).<br>
Please note that we may not be able to respond after the deadline.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Baggage Tracing
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Once you have completed the claim, this system offers you the ability to obtain the latest information regarding the location of your delayed baggage online.<br>
To use this service, you will need the reference number given upon arrival or&nbsp;received upon applying via self service along with your family name. The reference number is different from the baggage tag number. If you do not have a reference number, contact the service desk at the arrival airport.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>You also can check the current status yourself by entering your reference number at the <strong><a href="https://mybag.aero/ana/managemybag" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">Baggage Tracing System<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong> website.</p>
<ul>
<li>This service is provided only in English.</li>
<li>Only passengers on ANA Group-operated flights (Excluding flights whose flight number begins with NQ) may use this system.</li>
<li>If you connected to a flight of another airline after taking an ANA flight and your baggage did not arrive at the final destination, you should contact the airline you boarded last (the operating airline in the event of a codeshare flight).</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Baggage Return
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>We will clear customs on your behalf and deliver your found baggage to your designated location.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Contents Declaration
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>To expedite the search for your items, you may be asked to provide details about the contents of the baggage. We may ask you to fill out a <a href="/www2/pdf/travel-informtion/missing_property_questionnaire.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf"><strong>Missing Property Questionnaire</strong><img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a>. This constitutes important information which will be used for reference when issuing compensation.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Compensation
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>In the rare event that your baggage is not found, ANA will issue compensation 30 to 45 days after your arrival in accordance with the <a href="/en/us/conditions-of-carriage/"><strong>International Conditions of Carriage</strong></a>.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

                    </div>
                </div><!-- / cp-tab-contents -->
            
                
                <div id="anchor-forgotten-wrong-baggage-contents" class="cp-tab-contents" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="anchor-forgotten-wrong-baggage">
                    
                    <div class="res-contents cp-container">
                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 aem-Grid--large--12 aem-Grid--medium--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Baggage Forgotten, Wrong Baggage Picked Up, Left-Behind Items
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn--offset--medium--0 aem-GridColumn--medium--none aem-GridColumn--offset--large--0 aem-GridColumn--large--none aem-GridColumn--medium--12 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12 aem-GridColumn--large--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>After arrival, each passenger must pick up their checked baggage at baggage claim by confirming the numbers on the baggage claim tags.</p>
<p>If you leave the airport without picking up your baggage or with someone else's baggage by mistake, please contact the arrival airport immediately. (See Airport Contact Information above.)</p>
<p>This information applies to airports within Japan. If you arrived at an airport outside Japan, please inquire with the arrival airport, as procedures may vary depending on the airport.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Left-Behind Baggage
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Retrieving left-behind baggage requires that the baggage clear Customs. You have two options for achieving this:</p>
<p><strong>Return to the Airport to Clear Customs Yourself</strong></p>
<p>If you are clearing customs by yourself (for urgent cases), please contact the arrival airport and return to the airport with your passport. An ANA staff member will show you the way to the Customs office. Your baggage will clear customs in your attendance and the baggage will then be returned to you.</p>
<p><strong>Use an Agent to Clear Customs for You</strong></p>
<p>ANA can act as your agent in passing through Customs, if desired, but be aware that this requires several days.</p>
<p><strong>Required Documents</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>A copy of your passport (the photograph page and the page stamped at the time of entry into the country).<ul>
<li>Note: We may not be able to handle your request if the copy is not sufficiently clear.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A completed <a href="/www2/pdf/travel-informtion/application_en.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf"><strong>Customs Clearance Application/Authorization Letter</strong><img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a>.<ul>
<li>Only the original authorization letter will be accepted; no copies.</li>
<li>Please bring required documents directly to the airport, or send them by postal mail.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Pickup by a customs agent can typically be performed the day your documentation is received. ANA will contact you regarding delivery times. In principle, customers will be responsible for any shipping charges. Your baggage will be delivered to a place of your choosing with payment due on delivery.</p>
<ul>
<li>If you notice after arriving on a flight not operated by ANA that you left your baggage behind, please inquire with the airline on which you arrived.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h4 class="type--header-4 ">
              
                Left behind item on an aircraft
              
            </h4>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>If your item was left on an aircraft, please contact us using the&nbsp;<strong><a href="https://acis-cs-ana.web.app/lostitem/int-en" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">Inquiry Form<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong>.</p>
<p>If we find the item, we will deliver it to you promptly. Please note at you will be asked to pay delivery costs.</p>
<p>Items found in an airport facility and not in the cabin may be stored by the airport managing company or at a police station. Please contact the airport to inquire about your item.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

    
</div>

                    </div>
                </div><!-- / cp-tab-contents -->
