<div class="contents responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div id="wrap-container" class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h2 class="type--header-2 ">
              
                Items With Conditions Attached to Their Carry-on or Check-in (International Flights)
              
            </h2>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>This page contains information on the restrictions in place for all routes. There are certain items that cannot be carried on board or checked in for international flights. Please be sure to check which items this applies to before coming to the airport.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1607 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1607 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents">
        <div class="jq-accordion">
            
            <div></div>
        </div>
        <div class="content-wrapper cmp-accordion" data-cmp-single-expansion="false" role="list">
            <div class="jq-accordion cmp-accordion__item" data-cmp-hook-accordion="item" data-cmp-expanded="" role="listitem">
                
                
                
                    <div aria-controls="anchor-information" class="accordion-head cmp-accordion__button--expanded" data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-expanded="true">
                        <h3 class="cmp-accordion__title">Notes</h3>
                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="anchor-information" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--expanded" aria-hidden="false"><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid">

        <div class="res-contents ana2_bgcolor_ui-02">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ana2_color_text-01">
        <ul>
<li>If a codeshare flight or flight operated by another airline is included in the itinerary, the baggage rules of the other airline may apply.</li>
<li>When traveling on Japanese domestic sectors using a ticket for which the International Conditions of Carriage apply, the baggage rules for international flights will apply.</li>
<li>Please be advised that in the event that it is impossible to confirm whether or not an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>
<li>Some countries and regions may place restrictions on the carry-on and check-in of items other than those mentioned.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
</div>
                
            </div>

            
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<!-- ANA-1607 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        <div id="be-contents-sync" class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Items Which Are Not Permitted to Be Checked In or Carried on Board
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Please note that it is prohibited by law to check in or carry on dangerous goods on board. (Depending on the laws and regulations of the relevant country, violation may be subject to legal penalties or fines.)<br>
Please discard of any dangerous goods you are carrying with you in the box for abandoned property which is placed in front of the security checkpoint.<br>
Explosives (fireworks, firecrackers, unexploded bombs, etc.), flammable substances (including a large quantity of matches, lighter fuel, camping/household stoves, and alcoholic beverages containing more than 70 % alcohol), compressed gases (including gas cartridges for gas cartridge stoves, oxygen canisters for sports, and dust-proof sprays), toxic substances (including insecticides), corrosive substances*, radioactive substances, ferromagnetic substances, oxidizing substances*, harmful or irritating materials, and any other items that may endanger or cause trouble for the aircraft itself and/or the persons and items on board it.</p>
<p style="margin-left: 40.0px;">* Bleach is considered to be either a corrosive or oxidizing substance, and is therefore not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1612 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1612 -->

            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Typical Examples of Dangerous Goods
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ana2_color_text-01">
        <ul>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.mlit.go.jp/common/001425422.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf">Please see here for typical examples of dangerous goods which are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board (Homepage of Japan's Ministry of Land, Infrastructure, Transport and Tourism).<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a></strong></li>
<li><strong><a href="https://nettv.gov-online.go.jp/prg/prg12075.html" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">What can I take on board an aircraft? Which items aren't allowed? (Japanese Government Internet TV)<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong></li>
<li><strong><a href="/dom/checkin/rules/pdf/221006/examples.pdf" target="_blank" class="icon-pdf">Information about Dangerous Goods (PDF format /&nbsp;0.98 MB)<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_pdf.png" class="ico-pdf-img" alt="Open PDF in a new window."></a></strong></li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1607 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1607 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents">
        <div class="jq-accordion">
            
            <div></div>
        </div>
        <div class="content-wrapper cmp-accordion" data-cmp-single-expansion="false" role="list">
            <div class="jq-accordion cmp-accordion__item" data-cmp-hook-accordion="item" role="listitem">
                
                
                
                    <div aria-controls="anchor-Oil-filled" class="accordion-head" data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-expanded="false">
                        <h4 class="cmp-accordion__title">Oil-filled pocket warmers</h4>
                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="anchor-Oil-filled" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--hidden" aria-hidden="true"><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Oil-filled pocket warmers are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board, as they use flammable liquid as fuel which falls under the dangerous goods regulations.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-0102-1 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-0102-1-->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cp-container cp-list-container">
        <ul role="list" class="list-ul list-style-asterisk list-mt-normal">
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                Although the inner configuration of an oil-filled pocket warmer is similar to that of an oil lighter with absorbent cotton, carry-on of one lighter per person is specially permitted in the dangerous goods regulations provided that it is a lighter used for smoking.
                
            </li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-0102-1 -->


    

</div>

        
    </div>
</div>

</div>
</div>
                
            </div>
<div class="jq-accordion cmp-accordion__item" data-cmp-hook-accordion="item" role="listitem">
                
                
                
                    <div aria-controls="anchor-Gas-cartridges" class="accordion-head" data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-expanded="false">
                        <h4 class="cmp-accordion__title">Gas Cartridges / Insecticides and Pesticides / Fireworks and Firecrackers</h4>
                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="anchor-Gas-cartridges" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--hidden" aria-hidden="true"><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Gas Cartridges for Camping
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Stoves are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board unless it is possible to check that no gas is remaining in the main body of the stove.<br>
Gas canisters and gas cartridges are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Insecticides and Pesticides
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Insecticides and pesticides are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board regardless of their amount.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

    </div>

            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Items With Conditions Attached to Their Carry-on or Check-in (International Flights)

<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>This page contains information on the restrictions in place for all routes. The items listed here can be placed inside carry-on baggage or checked baggage as long as certain conditions are met.</p>

    </div>

                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>

    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ana2_color_text-01">
        <ul>
<li>If a codeshare flight or flight operated by another airline is included in the itinerary,&nbsp;<strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/codeshare/">the baggage rules of the other airline</a></strong>&nbsp;may apply.</li>
<li>When traveling on Japanese domestic sectors using a ticket for which the International Conditions of Carriage apply, the baggage rules for international flights will apply.</li>
<li>Please check the information about hazardous chemicals on the SDS (Safety Data Sheet), the relevant instruction manuals, etc. in advance to make sure that there are no dangerous goods among your belongings.</li>
<li>Please be advised that in the event that it is impossible to confirm whether or not an item can be transported by airplane before the departure time, the request for transport may be rejected.</li>
<li>Some countries and regions may place&nbsp;<strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/restricted-prohibited/restrictions/">restrictions on the carry-on and check-in</a></strong>&nbsp;of items other than those mentioned below.</li>

<li>* Lighter fuel and refills (gas/oil) are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</li>
<li>*&nbsp;Lithium battery-powered lighters that do not have a function to prevent accidental activation are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</li>

            </h6>

    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>According to IATA Dangerous Goods Regulations, for cosmetics (hairsprays or antiperspirant sprays), medicine/medicinal products (sterilization/disinfection sprays or cooling sprays), and sprays for sporting equipment and daily use (excluding those containing flammable and poisonous gases), 2 kg or 2 liters per person are permitted to be checked in or carried on board in containers of up to 0.5 kg or 0.5 liters.</p>
<p><em>However, even if the liquid item is within the carry-on limits permitted by the regulations, it may not be possible to bring it on board depending on restrictions imposed on the carry-on of liquids for international flights. For further details, please see <strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/carry-on/">the information on carry-on baggage restrictions</a></strong>.</em></p>

<li>* When checking in non-radioactive cosmetics or drugs and sprays for sporting equipment or daily use together, their combined amount must not exceed 2 kg or 2 liters.</li>

<div class="jq-accordion cmp-accordion__item" data-cmp-hook-accordion="item" role="listitem">
                
                
                
                    <div aria-controls="anchor-Lithium-ion-batteries" class="accordion-head" data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-expanded="false">
                        <h4 class="cmp-accordion__title">General Electronic Devices with Built-in or Attached Lithium Batteries</h4>
                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="anchor-Lithium-ion-batteries" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--hidden" aria-hidden="true"><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Lithium battery is the generic term for lithium-metal batteries and lithium ion batteries.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                General Electronic Devices with Built-in or Attached Lithium Batteries
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Handling differs depending to the watt-hour rating (Wh).</p>
<p>If the watt-hour rating (Wh) is not indicated, please use the following formula to confirm it.</p>
<p>Watt-hour rating (Wh) = rated capacity (Ah) × rated voltage (V)</p>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* 1000mAh = 1Ah<br>
Example) 27Wh = (2500mAh ÷ 1000) × 10.8V</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Product examples
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul>
<li>cell phones</li>
<li>battery chargers for cell phones</li>
<li>wireless radios</li>
<li>transceivers</li>
<li>laptop computers</li>
<li>digital cameras</li>
<li>mobile terminals</li>
<li>portable copiers</li>
<li>printers</li>
<li>hand-held terminals</li>
<li>electronic book readers</li>
<li>mobile game devices</li>
<li>camera equipment</li>
<li>Wireless earphones</li>
</ul>
<p>etc.</p>
<p style="margin-left: 40.0px;">* Electric vehicles (hoverboards, electric skateboards, self-balancing scooters, etc.) are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board due to safety reasons.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Electronic device
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Lithium-metal batteries containing no more than 2 g of lithium and lithium ion batteries with a watt-hour rating of no more than 160 Wh can be checked in or carried on board</p>
<p>(Notes)<br>
Please take the measures below for checking in electronic devices containing lithium batteries as checked baggage.</p>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* Turn off the power of the device completely. (Sleep mode is not allowed.)</li>
<li>* Please protect the device by packing it in a sturdy suitcase or thick fabric. (To prevent fires from accidental operation or damage)</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Spare Batteries
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Spare batteries cannot be transported on their own as they must be transported together with the actual electronic device.</p>
<p>Lithium-metal batteries containing no more than&nbsp;2 g&nbsp;of lithium and lithium ion batteries with a watt-hour rating of no more than&nbsp;100 Wh&nbsp;can be carried on board. They are not permitted to be checked in.</p>
<p>Up to two lithium ion batteries with a watt-hour rating exceeding&nbsp;100 Wh&nbsp;but of no more than&nbsp;160 Wh&nbsp;can be carried on board. They are not permitted to be checked in.</p>
<p style="margin-left: 40.0px;">* Battery chargers with a lithium ion battery for cell phones are handled as spare batteries.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Short circuit prevention measures
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Please take measures such as putting the batteries in their original retail packaging or insulating the terminals (taping over exposed terminals or placing each battery in a separate plastic bag or protective pouch).</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Request for batteries in general
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>For safety reasons, passengers with spare batteries other than lithium-metal batteries and lithium ion batteries (such as nickel-metal hydride, nickel-cadmium, and alkaline manganese batteries) should take the necessary steps to prevent them from short circuiting before taking them on board the aircraft.</p>

    </div>

<!--/ANA-1604 -->

                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>

    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">

<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Items with a non-removable lithium battery are not permitted to be checked in or carried on board.</p>
<p>Smart baggage with a removable lithium battery can be checked in and carried on board.<br>
The removed lithium battery should be carried on board. If you would like to carry smart baggage on board, please confirm the size and weight restrictions for carry-on baggage.</p>
<p>It will be possible to check in and carry on board lithium-metal batteries with a lithium content of 0.3 g or less and lithium-ion batteries with a watt-hour rating of 2.7 Wh or less. (This also includes non-removable lithium batteries.)</p>
<ul class="none-style">
<li>* For information about the capacities and quantities for removable lithium batteries, please see (<strong><a href="#anchor-Lithium-ion-batteries">General Electronic Devices with Built-in or Attached Lithium Batteries</a></strong>).</li>

<p>Smart baggage refers to baggage containing integrated batteries, which allow for the charging of electronic devices and other functions.</p>

<p>Up to one battery per person with a watt-hour rating (Wh) exceeding&nbsp;160 Wh&nbsp;but of&nbsp;no more than&nbsp;300&nbsp;Wh&nbsp;is allowed to be carried on board. It is not permitted to be checked in.</p>

        <p>Out of consideration for other passengers, the use of electronic cigarettes, electronic pipes, electronic cigarettes, personal vaporizers, electronic nicotine delivery devices, and other smoking devices that do not use fire (including those that do not emit smoke) is also prohibited on board ANA Group-operated&nbsp;flights.             <li role="listitem" class="bullet">

<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul class="none-style">
<li>* There are no restrictions on alcoholic beverages with an alcohol content of 24% or less.</li>
<li>* The alcoholic beverages must be stored in the container in which they were sold.</li>
<li>* Even if an alcoholic beverage is within the carry-on limits permitted by the regulations, it may not be possible to bring it on board depending on restrictions imposed on the carry-on of liquids for international flights. For further details, please see&nbsp;<strong><a href="/en/us/travel-information/baggage-information/carry-on/">the information on carry-on baggage restrictions.</a></strong></li>
</ul>

    </div>

<!--/ANA-1604 -->

    </div>

<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">

        <p>Up to 2.5 kg per person of items used for cooling perishable goods can be checked in or carried on board.</p>

                        <div class="arrow down"></div>

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">

<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Only one avalanche rescue backpack per person can be carried on board or checked in. The amount of explosive used must be no more than 200 mg, and the type of compressed gas used must be neither flammable nor toxic.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <ul class="none-style">
<li>* The backpack must be packed in such a manner that it cannot be accidentally activated, and measures must be taken to ensure that the airbag inside it does not inflate.</li>
<li>* The airbag inside the backpack must have pressure release valves.</li>
<li>* Please provide explanatory documents to prove that conditions are met.</li>
<li>* Spare cylinders cannot be carried on board or checked in.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>

        <p>Lithium-ion batteries rated 160 Wh or lower are allowed in both carry-on baggage and checked baggage.<br>
Please completely turn off the power to the device, and take measures to prevent fires caused by accidental use or damage.</p>

        <p>Battery-operated underwater torches (lights for scuba diving) or soldering irons, etc.</p>
<ul>
<li>Items with their battery removed to prevent accidental operation during transport can be checked in or carried on board without restrictions.</li>
</ul>

    </div>

                        <div class="arrow down"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="anchor-Heat-producing-articles" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--hidden" aria-hidden="true"><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid">

        <div class="res-contents ">
    
    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h5 class="type--header-5 ">
              
                Transportation of experimental drugs
              
            </h5>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>Experimental drugs in development can only be checked in or carried on board if the following conditions are met.<br>
As it may take some time for the security check and necessary confirmation, please arrive at the airport with adequate time to spare.</p>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Conditions
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-0102-1 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-0102-1-->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cp-container cp-list-container">
        <ul role="list" class="list-ul list-style-hyphen list-mt-normal">
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                The passenger has a document stating that it is an experimental drug.
                
            </li>
        
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                There is no "three-leaf mark" indicating that the drug is radioactive on the outer container.
                
            </li>
        
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                Security check standards* established in the Civil Aeronautics Act of Japan are met.
                
                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="ANA-0102-2 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-0102-2 -->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <ul role="list" class="res-contents list-ul list-style-asterisk list-mt-normal">
        <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
            
            Liquid experimental drugs need to undergo a liquid inspection or will be opened for inspection in order to allow them to be carried on board. Please note that if the container cannot be opened, the item may not be permitted to be checked in or carried on board.
            
        </li>
    </ul>
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-0102-2 -->


    

</div>

    
</div>

                
            </li>
        
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                The quantity restrictions are 0.5 L or 0.5 kg per container, and 2 L or 2 kg per person.
                
            </li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-0102-1 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h6 class="type--header-6 ">
              
                Security Checks for Experimental Drugs
              
            </h6>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>

</tr><tr><td>Travel agency</td>
<td>Travel agency where ticket was purchased</td>
</tr></tbody></table>

  </div>
  <!-- //ANA-3022 -->


    
</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--bullet">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Depending on the currency used for the payment, a refund may not be possible outside the country of purchase due to currency restrictions.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Refunds made outside Japan may be made by check.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>The refund will be made in the local currency.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        </ul>
    <!-- // ANA-3014 -->


    






</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--note-num">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
				
                    <span class="asw-list__bullet">
                        <span class="asw-list__bullet-note">*</span>
                        1
                    </span>
                    <div class="asw-list__content">
                        <p>For purchases made with large sums of cash (including purchases using ANA travel vouchers), refund requests cannot be accepted at airport counters. For further details, please contact ANA in Japan by phone.</p>

                        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                    </div>
                
            </li>
        </ul>

	<!-- ANA-3013 -->
    
		<div class="asw-headline asw-headline--head4">
			<h4 class="asw-headline__title">
				
					Validity for Refund
					
				
			</h4>
            
		</div>
    
    
    
    
	<!-- // ANA-3013 -->


    
</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text asw-text--label1">
      <p><span style="color: #006ba4;">Tickets</span></p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>Refund requests are accepted within one year and 30 days of the date of the first flight sector on the ticket (or the date of issue if unused), after confirmation of the e-Ticket Itinerary Receipt and the submission of the necessary information.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text asw-text--label1">
      <p><span style="color: rgb(0,107,164);">EMD</span></p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>Refund requests are accepted within one year and 30 days of the relevant EMD issuance date, upon submission of the necessary information.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3013 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3013 -->
    
		<div class="asw-headline asw-headline--head4">
			<h4 class="asw-headline__title">
				
					Refund Amount
					
				
			</h4>
            
		</div>
    
    
    
    
	<!-- // ANA-3013 -->


    
</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text asw-text--label1">
      <p><span style="color: #006ba4;">Tickets</span></p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p><strong>Before first flight sector:</strong> refunds are calculated by subtracting the relevant handling fees from the total amount paid includes taxes/fees (Passenger Service Facility Charge etc.).</p>
<p><strong>After first flight sector:</strong> the refund is calculated by subtracting the handling fees, the fares for used sectors, and the taxes/fees (Passenger Service Facility Charge etc.) for unused sectors from the total amount paid.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--annotation">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Refunds may not be available for some fares.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Depending on the country and itinerary, the handling fees for changes, refunds and cancellations stipulated in the relevant fare rules may be subject to separate taxation.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>In case of a refund request after changing the reservation, the strictest fare rules among the changed fares will apply.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        </ul>
    <!-- // ANA-3014 -->


    






</div>

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->

  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>If cancellation charges have been specified, the refund amount will be calculated by subtracting the designated charges from the amount paid.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

	<!-- ANA-3013 -->

			<h4 class="asw-headline__title">
				
					Refund Methods and Processing Time
					
				
			</h4>
            
		</div>
    
    
    
    
	<!-- // ANA-3013 -->


    
</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text asw-text--label1">
      <p><span style="color: #006ba4;">When paid by credit card</span></p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>Refunds will be made via the company of the credit card used for purchase.<br>
This may take up to one to two months depending on when the refund request is received, and the closing date and refund processing procedure conditions of the applicable credit card company.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--annotation">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>In some cases, the ticket purchase and the refund request are processed first and the service fee is charged at a later time, while in other cases the ticket purchase is processed first, and the ticket amount, less the handling fee, is refunded at a later time. For details, please contact your credit card company.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Extra time may be necessary if coordination with other airline companies is required.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        </ul>

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text asw-text--label1">
      <p><span style="color: #006ba4;">When paid in cash</span></p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>Cash will be deposited into your bank account (any bank transfer fees are borne by the passenger), or a check will be issued (may apply to certain areas outside Japan upon ticket issuance).</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--annotation">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>As a general rule, the person who is named as the passenger on the ticket will receive the refund. For identification purposes, you may be asked to present your ANA Mileage Club membership number, an official identification document, or an authorization letter.</p>
<p>Official identification documents: Passport, driver's license, insurance card, residence card (for non-Japanese nationals residing in Japan), ward/city/town/village residence card, pension booklet, etc.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        </ul>
    <!-- // ANA-3014 -->


    






</div>
<div class="ANA-3010 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

  <!-- ANA-3010 -->
  
    <div class="asw-text">
      <p>The refund will be issued to the specified account within approximately 10 days after the refund is processed.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-3014 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
	<!-- ANA-3014 -->
		<ul class="asw-list asw-list--annotation">
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Refunds may take more than 10 days in some cases, especially around the year-end/New Year holiday period.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Processing time may even be longer in certain situations, such as during the failure of financial institution systems, or when numerous flights have been canceled due to inclement weather.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>
        
            <li class="asw-list__item">
				
                    <p>Extra time may be necessary if coordination with other airline companies is required.</p>

                    


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

                
				
            </li>

					Involuntary Changes and Refunds due to Irregularities beyond ANA's control (such as bad weather)
					
				
			</h2>
            
		</div>

      <p>Customers who experience delays and cancellations which are caused by circumstances beyond ANA's control *1 can receive refunds or be rebooked onto another ANA-operated flight.<br>
Please note that there may be cases in which customer requests cannot be fulfilled due to terms related to the ticket type or flight transfer process.</p>

    </div>
  

  

  
  <!--/ANA-3010 -->

                        1
                    </span>

<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    
    
</div>

            </li>

                Cancellations / Refunds (International Flights)

    <div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--small--12 aem-Grid--default--12 aem-Grid--medium--12 ">
        
        <div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h2 class="type--header-2 ">
              
                Information on Delay and Cancellation at the Airport on the Departure Day
              
            </h2>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>
<div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<!-- ANA-1604 -->
<div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>There may be cases when flights are delayed, cancelled or diverted on the departure day due to various reasons such as congestion at the airport and bad weather. In such instances, we strive to provide accurate information on the situation as quickly as possible via airport information displays and announcements, on the ANA website and through the ANA Reservation and Customer Service Center.</p>
<ul>
<li>If you are unable to reach your final destination on your scheduled date of arrival due to a major flight delay or cancellation attributable to ANA, we will cover the cost of accommodation/public transport/etc.</li>
<li>If a flight is delayed or canceled due to events beyond our control such as bad weather, we will assist you with making arrangements for accommodation and so on to the extent that we can. Please note, however, that you will be responsible for covering the costs incurred.</li>
</ul>

    </div>
</div>


    

<!--/ANA-1604 -->
</div>
<div class="ANA-0102-1 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
    <!-- ANA-0102-1-->
    <div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
    <div class="res-contents cp-container cp-list-container">
        <ul role="list" class="list-ul list-style-asterisk list-mt-narrow">
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                Please note that this information pertains to the flight irregularities on the day of departure, and it does not apply to cancellations or schedule changes that happen prior to the departure date.
                
            </li>
        
            <li role="listitem" class="bullet">
				
                The respective certificates can be downloaded from <strong><a href="/fs/certificate/int/en/" target="_blank" class="icon-blank">Issue Certificate of Delay/Cancellation/Diversion<img src="/common-layout/images/icon_blank_BLU.png" class="ico-blank-img" alt="Opens in a new window.In the case of an external site,it may or may not meet accessibility guidelines."></a></strong> on the ANA website.<br>
Please note that certificates can only be issued for ANA-operated flights. Certificates for international codeshare flights operated by a partner airline are not available through this service.
                
            </li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-0102-1 -->


    

</div>

    <!-- ANA-1603 -->
    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">
        
            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">
              
                Coverage of Costs
              
            </h3>
        
    </div>
    <!--/ANA-1603 -->


    

</div>

    <div class="table-responsive res-contents">
      <table class="table"><thead><tr><th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Reason for Delay, Cancellation or Similar Event</strong></th>
<th scope="col" style="text-align: left;" class="text-nowrap vtop"><strong>Coverage of Costs</strong></th>
</tr></thead>
<tbody><tr><td>Reasons attributable to ANA</td>
<td>ANA to cover cost of accommodation/public transport/etc.</td>
</tr><tr><td>Bad weather, airport congestion and other unexpected events</td>
<td>Passenger to cover cost of accommodation/public transport/etc.</td>
</tr></tbody></table>

    </div><!-- / table-responsive -->

    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">
        <p>If your flight is delayed or canceled due to a reason attributable to ANA, we will reimburse the subsequent costs incurred for accommodation/public transport/etc. in accordance with the parameters established by ANA.</p>
<ul>
<li>The original receipts must be submitted for reimbursements. Copies are not accepted.</li>
</ul>

    </div>

        	<script type="text/javascript" src="/www2/js/travel-information/cancellation-and-delays/cancellation-and-delays_en.js"></script><div class="ANA-1606 responsivegrid aem-GridColumn--default--none aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12 aem-GridColumn--offset--default--0"><div class="res-contents "><div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--default--12 "><div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">    <!-- ANA-1603 -->    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">Contingency Plan for Lengthy Tarmac Delays</h3>    </div>    <!--/ANA-1603 --></div><div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1604 --><div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;"><div class="res-contents cmp-text "><p>This contingency plan for lengthy tarmac delays is applicable to flights operated by All Nippon Airways Co., Ltd. (ANA) and by its subsidiary Air Japan Co., Ltd. (AJX) and has been adopted pursuant to the requirements of section 259.4 of the regulations of the U.S. Department of Transportation (DOT).<br>For all flights, which depart from or arrive at U.S. airports, we will not allow the aircraft to remain on the tarmac without an opportunity for passengers to deplane for more than 4 hours in the case of arrivals or flights that are diverted. For departures, we will not allow the aircraft to remain on the tarmac without requesting to return to a suitable disembarkation point.*</p></div></div><!--/ANA-1604 --></div><div class="ANA-0102-1 aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-0102-1--><div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;"><div class="res-contents cp-container cp-list-container"><ul role="list" class="list-ul list-style-asterisk list-mt-narrow">    <li role="listitem" class="bullet">        The following cases, however, are excluded: The pilot-in-command (PIC) determines the aircraft should not leave where they are on the tarmac to disembark passengers for safety or security reasons, or Air Traffic Control (ATC) advises the PIC that returning to the gate or another place for disembarkation would significantly disrupt airport operations.    </li></ul></div></div><!--/ANA-0102-1 --></div><div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1604 --><div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;"><div class="res-contents cmp-text "><p>We will make the following reasonable efforts to provide convenient and comfortable service to all customers in the event that a flight is delayed.</p></div></div><!--/ANA-1604 --></div><div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1604 --><div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;"><div class="res-contents cmp-text "><ol><li>Provide adequate food and potable water no later than 2 hours from the start of the tarmac delay, unless the PIC determines that safety or security precludes such service.</li><li>Ensure that operable lavatory facilities and adequate medical assistance, if needed, are available.</li><li>Provide passengers on the aircraft status updates during the tarmac delay, if the tarmac delay exceeds 30 minutes, and thereafter as ANA and AJX deems appropriate.</li><li>Provide passengers on the aircraft notification that they have the opportunity to deplane, if that opportunity exists.</li></ol></div></div><!--/ANA-1604 --></div><div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1604 --><div class="ana2-margin-top-S3" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;"><div class="res-contents cmp-text "><ul><li>We will make reasonable efforts to comply with this plan in the event of a diversion to any other U.S. airport.</li><li>We have committed sufficient resources to implement this plan and we have coordinated this plan with airport authorities (including terminal facility operators, U.S. Customs and Border Protection, and the Transportation Security Administration) at all U.S. airports that we serve including regular civilian diversion airports that are defined by DOT to be a "non-hub" or larger airport.</li><li>Services for codeshare flights are offered according to the standards of the operating airlines.</li></ul></div></div><!--/ANA-1604 --></div></div></div></div><div class="ANA-1603 title aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">    <!-- ANA-1603 -->    <div class="ana2-margin-top-L1" style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">            <h3 class="type--header-3 ">Allowing Reservations to be Canceled Without Penalty</h3>    </div>    <!--/ANA-1603 --></div><div class="ANA-1604 text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><!-- ANA-1604 --><div style="padding-left:15px;padding-right:15px;">    <div class="res-contents cmp-text ">        <p>A ticketed reservation made via ANA SKY WEB U.S., ANA Customer Service Center in the U.S. or ticketing counters at US airports served by ANA may be cancelled without penalty within 24 hours after the issuance of the ticket, except for reservations made within one week of departure, which may be cancelled without penalty only if permitted by applicable fare rules.</p><ul><li>Refunds must be requested through the ANA Customer Service Center in the U.S.</li><li>As for award tickets, expired miles cannot be refunded.</li></ul>    </div></div><!--/ANA-1604 --></div></div></div></div>
